0                                  26522              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                   26523              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26524              Ÿ   OLDBILL -- Routine to write the old charging records, given       Ÿ
                                   26525              Ÿ     the new charging record.                                        Ÿ
                                   26526              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26527              Ÿ   This is for compatibility with the accounting system; the new     Ÿ
                                   26528              Ÿ   &WSMFBIL (type 171) records contain all the information the       Ÿ
                                   26529              Ÿ   billing information in one record.  The old &WSMFSYS (type 170)   Ÿ
                                   26530              Ÿ   records are produced here in the old format to allow the          Ÿ
                                   26531              Ÿ   existing accounting programs to run unchanged.                    Ÿ
                                   26532              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26533              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26534              Ÿ   This routine is straight forward. the new smf record              Ÿ
                                   26535              Ÿ   data structure has several sub-records, each one of               Ÿ
                                   26536              Ÿ   which generates three old SMF type records. (one for              Ÿ
                                   26537              Ÿ   milten, one for orvyl, and one for wylbur)  all we                Ÿ
                                   26538              Ÿ   do here is loop thru each component charge sub-record             Ÿ
                                   26539              Ÿ   creating and writing out the appropriate old type                 Ÿ
                                   26540              Ÿ   records.                                                          Ÿ
                                   26541              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26542              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26543              Ÿ   On entry:                                                         Ÿ
                                   26544              Ÿ     R1 - New SMF accounting record                                  Ÿ
                                   26545              Ÿ     R15- JCB ptr for user whose charge record is to be written      Ÿ
                                   26546              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26547              Ÿ   On exit:                                                          Ÿ
                                   26548              Ÿ     Old style SMF records written out from information obtained     Ÿ
                                   26549              Ÿ     from the new record.                                            Ÿ
                                   26550              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26551              Ÿ   Note:                                                             Ÿ
                                   26552              Ÿ     Any unrecognized new style accounting record is                 Ÿ
                                   26553              Ÿ     ignored (i.e., routine will not generate errors.).              Ÿ
                                   26554              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   26555              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»

                                   32000              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   32001              Ÿ  CHKACCT -- Routine to get/check the account, given the userid.     Ÿ
                                   32002              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   32003              Ÿ    On entry:                                                        Ÿ
                                   32004              Ÿ      R1,R0 - ACCT or ID loc,len                                     Ÿ
                                   32005              Ÿ      R15   - ptr to a 5 char return area (for "uuugg")              Ÿ
                                   32006              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   32007              Ÿ    On exit, R15 (and cc):                                           Ÿ
                                   32008              Ÿ      0 - account returned                                           Ÿ
                                   32009              Ÿ      nz- no ID for this account or account does not exist           Ÿ
                                   32010              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   32011              Ÿ  NOTE:                                                              Ÿ
                                   32012              Ÿ  GETACCT and CHKACCT are very similar.  They both take a            Ÿ
                                   32013              Ÿ  UserID or account as input.  They differ in that GETACCT           Ÿ
                                   32014              Ÿ  will not check to see if the account exists. CHKACCT does          Ÿ
                                   32015              Ÿ  check to see that the account exists.                              Ÿ
                                   32016              Ÿ     GETACCT of 'GG.UUU' returns r15=0                               Ÿ
                                   32017              Ÿ     CHKACCT of 'GG.UUU' returns r15=nz                              Ÿ
